***таскать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a> (3300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">taskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потаскать.html>потаска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry, to lug, to drag
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ежедневно.html>ежедне́вно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумка.html>су́мки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ježednévno <b>taskátʹ</b> tjažólyje súmki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry heavy bags every day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еле.html>е́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jéle nógi <b>taskátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be barely able to drag one's feet</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull along, to drag along
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:всюду.html>всю́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>собо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>taskátʹ</b> kovó-libo vsjúdu s sobój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take someone along everywhere</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">clothes or shoes, long or carelessly</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туфля.html>ту́фли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>taskáj</b> éti túfli v doždʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't wear [put on] these shoes when it rains</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">someone, causing pain; <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, by some body part</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>taskátʹ</b> kovó-libo za vólosy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull someone's hair</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to pull somebody by the hair</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pinch, to swipe, to pilfer, to filch</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is in the class of Russian abstract verbs. Its counterpart <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is a concrete verb.
</p>

***таскаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:таскаться.html>таска́ться</a> (15223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таскаться.html>таска́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">taskátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">потаска́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drag oneself <i>(to a place)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хо́чется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскаться.html>таска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne xóčetsja <b>taskátʹsja</b> tak dalekó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't feel like making such long trips</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приходиться.html>прихо́дится</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскаться.html>таска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:переполненный.html>перепо́лненной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:электричка.html>электри́чке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jej prixóditsja <b>taskátʹsja</b> na rabótu v perepólnennoj elektríčke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she has to take a tough ride in a packed commuter train to get to her office [place of work]</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскаться.html>таска́ешься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i začém ty tudá <b>taskáješʹsja</b> tak částo?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what's the big need for you to go there so often?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carry about, to carry along
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскаться.html>таска́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумка.html>су́мкой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on vsegdá <b>taskájetsja</b> s étoj súmkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he always carries this bag along; he never goes out without this bag</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gad about, to hang about
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскаться.html>таска́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:барин.html>ба́рам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>taskátʹsja</b> po báram</i> ― <span class="e-translation">gad about bars; barhop</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to follow, to trail along
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таскаться.html>таска́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́терью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on vsjó vrémja <b>taskájetsja</b> za máterʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he always follows [trails along behind] his mother</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run <i>(after)</i>, to dangle <i>(after)</i>, to chase <i>(after)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***тасовавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тасовать.html>тасова́вший</a> (26744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тат.html>тат</a> (19409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***татуировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:татуировать.html>татуи́ровать</a> (30591)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">tätowieren</i>; synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тат.html>тату́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tatú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:татуировать.html>татуи́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tatuírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:тать.html>тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tatĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tatь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thief</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***тачанка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тачанка.html>тача́нка</a> (27329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тачанка.html>тача́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tačánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тачанка.html>тача́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тачанка.html>тача́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тачанка.html>тача́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a type of spring cart (some military types were fitted with machine guns facing backwards during the Civil War in Russia 1917-1922)</li></ol>

***тачка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чка</a> (6730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тача́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tačátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stitch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  But compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">tačke</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">taczka</i>, etc.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">táčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wheelbarrow</li>
<li>shopping cart</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> taxi
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поймать.html>пойма́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pojmátʹ <b>táčku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to catch <b>a taxi</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> car</li></ol>

***тащить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a> (1912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">taščítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вытащить.html>вы́тащить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стащить.html>стащи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull, to drag, to haul
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Valentin Katayev, <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шади</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>трудо́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:громоздкий.html>громо́здкий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дилижанс.html>дилижа́нс</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Lóšadi s trudóm <b>taščíli</b> gromózdkij diližáns.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Horses <b>dragged</b> the unwieldy coach with difficulty.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carry (unwillingly or something heavy)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steal, to pinch
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стащить.html>стащи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">staščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>та́щит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́ли</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On opjátʹ <b>táščit</b> s zavóda detáli.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He's <b>stealing</b> parts from the plant again.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to please, to cause to revel
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> музо́н <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>та́щит</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot muzón menjá <b>táščit</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This music makes me <b>revel</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is in the class of Russian concrete verbs. Its counterpart <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таскать.html>таска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is an abstract verb.
</p>

</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="молодёжное"><a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мол</a>.</span> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="жаргон наркоманов">жарг. нарк.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́виться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:радовать.html>ра́довать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:доставлять.html>доставля́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствие</a>. <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***тащиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тащиться.html>тащи́ться</a> (8140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащиться.html>тащи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">taščítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потащиться.html>потащи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to trail along
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подол.html>подо́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тья</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тащиться.html>тащи́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podól plátʹja <b>taščílsja</b> po pólu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the skirt trailed on the floor</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drag oneself along
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еле.html>е́ле</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тащиться.html>тащи́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jéle <b>taščítʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">drag one's feet; be barely able to walk</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trail along <i>(behind)</i>, to follow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мной</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тащиться.html>та́щишься</a>?</b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što ty za mnoj <b>táščišʹsja?</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">why are you following me?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go, to drag oneself <i>(to a place)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неохота.html>неохо́та</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тащиться.html>тащи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>таку́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даль.html>даль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neoxóta <b>taščítʹsja</b> v takúju dalʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't feel at all like going that far</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get high <i>(on drugs)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">затащи́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zataščítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be in ecstasies <i>(about)</i>, to be sent into ecstasies, to be wild <i>(about)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">затащи́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zataščítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li>страд. <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

***таять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ять</a> (4047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tàjati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tájatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оттаять.html>отта́ять</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтаять.html>подта́ять</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растаять.html>раста́ять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to melt, to thaw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воск.html>воск</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vosk <b>tájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wax is melting</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рот.html>рту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tájatʹ</b> vo rtu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to melt in the mouth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to melt away, to wane, to dwindle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ют</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó síly <b>tájut</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his strength is dwindling (is on the wane)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>зву́ки</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ют</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zvúki <b>tájut</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sounds fade away</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́сы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ют</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">náši zapásy <b>tájut</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">our stocks are dwindling</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to waste away, to pine <i>(with)</i>, to languish (with)</li>
<li>to melt <i>(with)</i></li></ol>

***тварь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тварь.html>тварь</a> (3869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:тварь.html>тварь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tvarĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">item, object, creation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tvarь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тварь.html>тварь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tvarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тварь.html>тва́ри</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тварь.html>тва́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тварь.html>тва́рей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>creature, being, animal, beast, monster</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> someone mean, vile, worthless</li></ol>
